				<div class="elementor-post__text">
				<h3 class="elementor-post__title">
			<a href="https://www.outdoorapothecary.com/bat-boxes/">
				Build a Better Backyard with Bat Boxes			</a>
		</h3>

					<span class="elementor-post-date">
			January 13, 2026		</span>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-post__excerpt">
			<p>Discover why adding bat boxes to your garden creates balance, supports pollinators, and welcomes natural pest control—no chemicals, just wild harmony.</p>

( ( [ dropdownId, homeUrl ] ) => {
		const dropdown = document.getElementById( dropdownId );
		function onSelectChange() {
			setTimeout( () => {
				if ( 'escape' === dropdown.dataset.lastkey ) {
					return;
				}
				if ( dropdown.value ) {
					location.href = dropdown.value;
				}
			}, 250 );
		}
		function onKeyUp( event ) {
			if ( 'Escape' === event.key ) {
				dropdown.dataset.lastkey = 'escape';
			} else {
				delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
			}
		}
		function onClick() {
			delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
		}
		dropdown.addEventListener( 'keyup', onKeyUp );
		dropdown.addEventListener( 'click', onClick );
		dropdown.addEventListener( 'change', onSelectChange );
	} )( ["wp-block-archives-2","https://www.outdoorapothecary.com"] );
//# sourceURL=block_core_archives_build_dropdown_script
</script>

        const ads = document.querySelectorAll(".adthrive-ad iframe");

                if (typeof ad.width !== "undefined" && ad.width !== "1") {
                    ad.style.width = ad.width + "px";
            }
        })
    }
}, 50);
</script>
